\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Objects of class \char`\"{}\+Daidalus\char`\"{} compute the conflict bands using kinematic single-\/maneuver projections of the ownship and linear preditions of (multiple) traffic aircraft positions. The bands consist of ranges of guidance maneuvers\+: direction angles, horizontal speeds, vertical speeds, and altitude.

An assumption of the bands information is that the traffic aircraft do not maneuver. If the ownship immediately executes a NONE guidance maneuver, then the new path is conflict free (within a lookahead time of the parameter). If the ownship immediately executes a NEAR/\+MID/\+FAR guidance maneuver and no traffic aircraft maneuvers, then there will corresponding alert within the corresponding alerting level thresholds.

If recovery bands are set and the ownship is in a violation path, loss of separation recovery bands and recovery times are computed for each type of maneuver. If the ownship immediately executes a RECOVERY guidance maneuver, then the new path is conflict-\/free after the recovery time. Furthermore, the recovery time is the minimum time for which there exists a kinematic conflict-\/free maneuver in the future. 

Note that in the case of geodetic coordinates this version of bands performs an internal projection of the coordinates and velocities into the Euclidean frame (see Util/\+Projection). Accuracy may be reduced if the traffic plans involve any segments longer than Util.\+Projection.\+projection\+Conflict\+Range(lat,acc), and an error will be logged if the distance between traffic and ownship exceeds Util.\+Projection.\+projection\+Max\+Range() at any point in the lookahead range.

Disclaimers\+: The formal proofs of the core algorithms use real numbers, however these implementations use floating point numbers, so numerical differences could result. In addition, the geodetic computations include certain inaccuracies, especially near the poles.

The basic usage is 
\begin{DoxyPre}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus}{Daidalus}} daa = new \mbox{\hyperlink{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_ac822403869458467ebbcd28d7f6e339a}{Daidalus()}};
daa.loadFromFile(<configurationfile>);

...
daa.setOwnshipState(position of ownship, velocity of ownship);
daa.addTrafficState(position of (one) traffic aircraft, velocity of traffic);
daa.addTrafficState(position of (another) traffic aircraft, velocity of traffic);
...add other traffic aircraft...

for (int i = 0; i < daa.horizontalDirectionBandsLength(); i++ ) \{
   interval = daa.horizontalDirectionIntervalAt(i);
   lower\_ang = intrval.low;
   upper\_ang = intrval.up;
   regionType = daa.horizontalDirectionRegionAt(i);
   ..do something with this information..
\}

...similar for horizontal speed and vertical speed...
\end{DoxyPre}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::alert\+Level (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{ac\+\_\+idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes alert level of ownship and aircraft at index idx. The number 0 means no alert. A negative number means that aircraft index is not valid. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_adc2434ccd8a7bfacc0aa6ee63698c909}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_adc2434ccd8a7bfacc0aa6ee63698c909}} 
\index{larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}!alertLevel@{alertLevel}}
\index{alertLevel@{alertLevel}!larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{alertLevel()}{alertLevel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::alert\+Level (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{ac\+\_\+idx,  }\item[{int}]{turning,  }\item[{int}]{accelerating,  }\item[{int}]{climbing }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes alerting type of ownship and aircraft at index ac\+\_\+idx for current aircraft states. The number 0 means no alert. A negative number means that aircraft index is not valid. When the alerter object has been configured to consider ownship maneuvers, i.\+e., using spread values, the alerting logic could also use information about the ownship turning, accelerating, and climbing status as follows\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item turning \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0\+: ownship is turning left, turning \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0\+: ownship is turning right, turning = 0\+: do not make any turning assumption about the ownship.
\item accelerating \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0\+: ownship is decelerating, accelerating \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0\+: ownship is accelerating, accelerating = 0\+: do not make any accelerating assumption about the ownship.
\item climbing \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0\+: ownship is descending, climbing \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0\+: ownship is climbing, climbing = 0\+: do not make any climbing assumption about the ownship. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a0fbbfa2b883de9848d3081101de5243b}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a0fbbfa2b883de9848d3081101de5243b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::enable\+DTALogic\+With\+Horizontal\+Dir\+Recovery (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enable DAA Terminal Area (DTA) logic with horizontal direction recovery guidance, i.\+e., horizontal direction recovery is fully enabled, but vertical recovery blocks down resolutions when alert is higher than corrective. NOTE\+: When DTA logic is enabled, DAIDALUS automatically switches to DTA alerter and to special maneuver guidance, when aircraft enters DTA volume (depending on ownship-\/ vs intruder-\/centric logic). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a229904a00f6322bbeaf57a1568567494}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a229904a00f6322bbeaf57a1568567494}} 
\index{larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}!enableDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery@{enableDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery}}
\index{enableDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery@{enableDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery}!larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery()}{enableDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::enable\+DTALogic\+Without\+Horizontal\+Dir\+Recovery (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enable DAA Terminal Area (DTA) logic withou horizontal direction recovery guidance, i.\+e., horizontal direction recovery is disabled and vertical recovery blocks down resolutions when alert is higher than corrective. NOTE\+: When DTA logic is enabled, DAIDALUS automatically switches to DTA alerter and to special maneuver guidance, when aircraft enters DTA volume (depending on ownship-\/ vs intruder-\/centric logic). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_ae7307039c74ee42fb88b09ae9afb7d54}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_ae7307039c74ee42fb88b09ae9afb7d54}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::horizontal\+Contours (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::vector$<$ std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classlarcfm_1_1_position}{Position}} $>$ $>$ \&}]{blobs,  }\item[{int}]{ac\+\_\+idx,  }\item[{Bands\+Region\+::\+Region}]{region }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes horizontal contours contributed by aircraft at index idx, for given region. A contour is a list of points in counter-\/clockwise direction representing a polygon. Last point should be connected to first one. The computed polygon should only be used for display purposes since it\textquotesingle{}s merely an approximation of the actual contours defined by the violation and detection methods. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em blobs} & list of horizontal contours returned by reference. \\
\hline
{\em ac\+\_\+idx} & is the index of the aircraft used to compute the contours. \\
\hline
{\em region} & is the region used to compute detection. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::horizontal\+Hazard\+Zone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classlarcfm_1_1_position}{Position}} $>$ \&}]{haz,  }\item[{int}]{ac\+\_\+idx,  }\item[{bool}]{loss,  }\item[{bool}]{from\+\_\+ownship,  }\item[{Bands\+Region\+::\+Region}]{region }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes horizontal hazard zone around aircraft at index ac\+\_\+idx, for given region. A hazard zone is a list of points in counter-\/clockwise direction representing a polygon. Last point should be connected to first one. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em haz} & hazard zone returned by reference. \\
\hline
{\em ac\+\_\+idx} & is the index of the aircraft used to compute the contours. \\
\hline
{\em loss} & true means that the polygon represents the hazard zone. Otherwise, the polygon represents the hazard zone with an alerting time. \\
\hline
{\em from\+\_\+ownship} & true means ownship point of view. Otherwise, the hazard zone is computed from the intruder\textquotesingle{}s point of view. \\
\hline
{\em region} & is the region used to compute detection. NOTE\+: The computed polygon should only be used for display purposes since it\textquotesingle{}s merely an approximation of the actual hazard zone defined by the violation and detection methods. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::horizontal\+Speed\+Raw\+Resolution (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{dir }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Compute horizontal speed {\itshape raw} resolution maneuver. Raw resolution is the resolution without persistence @parameter dir is up (true)/down (false) of ownship current horizontal speed \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
horizontal speed resolution in internal units \mbox{[}m/s\mbox{]} in specified direction. Resolution maneuver is valid for lookahead time in seconds. Return NaN if there is no conflict, positive infinity if there is no up resolution, and negative infinity if there is no down resolution. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}!isEnabledDTALogicWithHorizontalDirRecovery@{isEnabledDTALogicWithHorizontalDirRecovery}}
\index{isEnabledDTALogicWithHorizontalDirRecovery@{isEnabledDTALogicWithHorizontalDirRecovery}!larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isEnabledDTALogicWithHorizontalDirRecovery()}{isEnabledDTALogicWithHorizontalDirRecovery()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::is\+Enabled\+DTALogic\+With\+Horizontal\+Dir\+Recovery (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Return true if DAA Terminal Area (DTA) logic is enabled with horizontal direction recovery guidance. If true, horizontal direction recovery is fully enabled, but vertical recovery blocks down resolutions when alert is higher than corrective. NOTE\+: When DTA logic is enabled, DAIDALUS automatically switches to DTA alerter and to special maneuver guidance, when aircraft enters DTA volume (depending on ownship-\/ vs intruder-\/centric logic). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a986e29a0119485c9a7c897947c3f8a21}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a986e29a0119485c9a7c897947c3f8a21}} 
\index{larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}!isEnabledDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery@{isEnabledDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery}}
\index{isEnabledDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery@{isEnabledDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery}!larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isEnabledDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery()}{isEnabledDTALogicWithoutHorizontalDirRecovery()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::is\+Enabled\+DTALogic\+Without\+Horizontal\+Dir\+Recovery (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Return true if DAA Terminal Area (DTA) logic is enabled without horizontal direction recovery guidance. If true, horizontal direction recovery is disabled and vertical recovery blocks down resolutions when alert is higher than corrective. NOTE\+: When DTA logic is enabled, DAIDALUS automatically switches to DTA alerter and to special maneuver guidance, when aircraft enters DTA volume (depending on ownship-\/ vs intruder-\/centric logic). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a48bbb2975d3ca5cc2cead02fa52b6d39}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a48bbb2975d3ca5cc2cead02fa52b6d39}}

\index{larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}!lastTrafficIndex@{lastTrafficIndex}}
\index{lastTrafficIndex@{lastTrafficIndex}!larcfm::Daidalus@{larcfm::Daidalus}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lastTrafficIndex()}{lastTrafficIndex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::last\+Traffic\+Index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
last traffic index. Every traffic aircraft has an index between 1 and last\+Traffic\+Index. The index 0 is reserved for the ownship. When last\+Traffic\+Index is 0, the ownship is set but no traffic aircraft has been set. When last\+Traffic\+Index is negative, ownship has not been set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Bands\+Region\+::\+Region larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::region\+Of\+Alert\+Level (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{ac\+\_\+idx,  }\item[{int}]{alert\+\_\+level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
region corresponding to a given alert level for a particular aircraft. This function first finds the alerter for this aircraft, based on ownship/intruder-\/centric logic, then returns the configured region for the alerter level. It returns UNKNOWN if the aircraft or the alert level are invalid.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void larcfm\+::\+Daidalus\+::set\+Alerting\+Logic (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{ownship\+\_\+centric }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set alerting logic to the value indicated by ownship\+\_\+centric. If ownship\+\_\+centric is true, alerting and guidance logic will use the alerter in ownship. \mbox{\hyperlink{classlarcfm_1_1_alerter}{Alerter}} in every intruder will be disregarded. If ownship\+\_\+centric is false, alerting and guidance logic will use the alerter in every intruder. \mbox{\hyperlink{classlarcfm_1_1_alerter}{Alerter}} in ownship will be disregarded. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a0b0ce7ba54f523b2d54a0fbb6c8671fc}\label{classlarcfm_1_1_daidalus_a0b0ce7ba54f523b2d54a0fbb6c8671fc}}

Compute vertical speed resolution maneuver for given direction. @parameter dir is up (true)/down (false) of ownship current vertical speed @parameter u units \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
vertical speed resolution in specified units \mbox{[}u\mbox{]} in specified direction. Resolution maneuver is valid for lookahead time in seconds. Return NaN if there is no conflict, positive infinity if there is no up resolution, and negative infinity if there is no down resolution. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
